    function CheckLevel()

    function CheckLevelBoss()
        if SelectBoss ~= 'Diamond [Lv. 750] [Boss]' then
            if SelectBoss ~= 'Jeremy [Lv. 850] [Boss]' then
                if SelectBoss ~= 'Fajita [Lv. 925] [Boss]' then
                    if SelectBoss ~= 'Don Swan [Lv. 1000] [Boss]' then
                        if SelectBoss ~= 'Smoke Admiral [Lv. 1150] [Boss]' then
                            if SelectBoss ~= 'Cursed Captain [Lv. 1325] [Raid Boss]' then
                                if SelectBoss ~= 'Awakened Ice Admiral [Lv. 1400] [Boss]' then

    function HopServer()
        local _PlaceId = game.PlaceId
        local u181 = {}
        local u182 = ''
        local _hour = os.date('!*t').hour

        function TPReturner()
            local v184

            if u182 ~= '' then
                v184 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. u182))
            else
                v184 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
            end
            if v184.nextPageCursor and (v184.nextPageCursor ~= 'null' and v184.nextPageCursor ~= nil) then
                u182 = v184.nextPageCursor
            end

            local v185, v186, v187 = pairs(v184.data)
            local v188 = 0

            while true do
                local v189

                v187, v189 = v185(v186, v187)

                if v187 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local v190 = true
                local u191 = tostring(v189.id)

                if tonumber(v189.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v189.playing) then
                    local v192, v193, v194 = pairs(u181)

                    while true do
                        local v195

                        v194, v195 = v192(v193, v194)

                        if v194 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v188 == 0 then
                            if tonumber(_hour) ~= tonumber(v195) then
                                pcall(function()
                                    u181 = {}

                                    table.insert(u181, _hour)
                                end)
                            end
                        elseif u191 == tostring(v195) then
                            v190 = false
                        end

                        v188 = v188 + 1
                    end

                    if v190 == true then
                        table.insert(u181, u191)
                        task.wait()
                        pcall(function()
                            wait()
                            game:GetService('TeleportService'):TeleportToPlaceInstance(_PlaceId, u191, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                        end)
                        wait(0.1)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function Teleport()
            while wait(1) do
                pcall(function()
                    TPReturner()

                    if u182 ~= '' then
                        TPReturner()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        Teleport()
    end
    function HOP()
        HopServer()
        HopServer()
        HopServer()
        HopServer()
        HopServer()

        while wait(0.2) do
            pcall(function()
                HopServer()

                if foundAnything ~= '' then
                    HopServer()
                end
            end)
        end
    end
    function Hop()
        local _PlaceId2 = game.PlaceId
        local u197 = {}
        local u198 = ''
        local _hour2 = os.date('!*t').hour

        function TPReturner()
            local v200

            if u198 ~= '' then
                v200 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId2 .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. u198))
            else
                v200 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId2 .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
            end
            if v200.nextPageCursor and (v200.nextPageCursor ~= 'null' and v200.nextPageCursor ~= nil) then
                u198 = v200.nextPageCursor
            end

            local v201, v202, v203 = pairs(v200.data)
            local v204 = 0

            while true do
                local v205

                v203, v205 = v201(v202, v203)

                if v203 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local v206 = true
                local u207 = tostring(v205.id)

                if tonumber(v205.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v205.playing) then
                    local v208, v209, v210 = pairs(u197)

                    while true do
                        local v211

                        v210, v211 = v208(v209, v210)

                        if v210 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v204 == 0 then
                            if tonumber(_hour2) ~= tonumber(v211) then
                                pcall(function()
                                    u197 = {}

                                    table.insert(u197, _hour2)
                                end)
                            end
                        elseif u207 == tostring(v211) then
                            v206 = false
                        end

                        v204 = v204 + 1
                    end

                    if v206 == true then
                        table.insert(u197, u207)
                        wait()
                        pcall(function()
                            wait()
                            game:GetService('TeleportService'):TeleportToPlaceInstance(_PlaceId2, u207, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                        end)
                        wait(4)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function Teleport()
            while wait() do
                pcall(function()
                    TPReturner()

                    if u198 ~= '' then
                        TPReturner()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        Teleport()
    end
    function isnil(p212)
        return p212 == nil
    end

    local function u214(p213)
        return math.floor(tonumber(p213) + 0.5)
    end

    Number = math.random(1, 1000000)

    function UpdatePlayerChams()
        local v215, v216, v217 = pairs(game:GetService('Players'):GetChildren())

        while true do
            local u218

            v217, u218 = v215(v216, v217)

            if v217 == nil then
                break
            end

            pcall(function()
                if not isnil(u218.Character) then
                    if ESPPlayer then
                        if isnil(u218.Character.Head) or u218.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                            u218.Character.Head['NameEsp' .. Number].TextLabel.Text = u218.Name .. ' | ' .. u214((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - u218.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M\nHealth : ' .. u214(u218.Character.Humanoid.Health * 100 / u218.Character.Humanoid.MaxHealth) .. '%'
                        else
                            local _BillboardGui = Instance.new('BillboardGui', u218.Character.Head)

                            _BillboardGui.Name = 'NameEsp' .. Number
                            _BillboardGui.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                            _BillboardGui.Size = UDim2.new(1, 200, 1, 30)
                            _BillboardGui.Adornee = u218.Character.Head
                            _BillboardGui.AlwaysOnTop = true

                            local _TextLabel11 = Instance.new('TextLabel', _BillboardGui)

                            _TextLabel11.Font = 'Code'
                            _TextLabel11.FontSize = 'Size14'
                            _TextLabel11.TextWrapped = true
                            _TextLabel11.Text = u218.Name .. ' \n' .. u214((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - u218.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M'
                            _TextLabel11.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                            _TextLabel11.TextYAlignment = 'Top'
                            _TextLabel11.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            _TextLabel11.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5

                            if u218.Team ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Team then
                                _TextLabel11.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255, 0, 0)
                            else
                                _TextLabel11.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 255, 0)
                            end
                        end
                    elseif u218.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                        u218.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number):Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    function UpdateChestEsp()

    function NoDodgeCool()
        if nododgecool then
            local v269 = next
            local v270, v271 = getgc()

            while true do
                local v272

                v271, v272 = v269(v270, v271)

                if v271 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Dodge and typeof(v272) == 'function' and getfenv(v272).script == game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Dodge then
                    local v273 = next
                    local v274, v275 = getupvalues(v272)

                    while true do
                        local v276

                        v275, v276 = v273(v274, v275)

                        if v275 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if tostring(v276) == '0.4' then
                            local v277 = v275

                            repeat
                                wait(0.1)
                                setupvalue(v272, v275, 0)
                            until not nododgecool

                            v275 = v277
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    function AutoHaki()
        if not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('HasBuso') then
            game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('Buso')
        end
    end
    function UnEquipWeapon(p278)
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(p278) then
            _G.NotAutoEquip = true

            wait(0.5)

            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(p278).Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack

            wait(0.1)

            _G.NotAutoEquip = false
        end
    end
    function EquipWeapon(p279)
        if not _G.NotAutoEquip and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(p279) then
            Tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(p279)

            wait(0.1)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(Tool)
        end
    end
    function GetDistance(p280)
        return math.floor((p280.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude)
    end
    function GetWeaponInventory(p281)
        local v282, v283, v284 = pairs(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('getInventory'))

        while true do
            local v285

            v284, v285 = v282(v283, v284)

            if v284 == nil then
                break
            end
            if type(v285) == 'table' and (v285.Type == 'Sword' and v285.Name == p281) then
                return true
            end
        end

        return false
    end

    end

    function tweenteleport(p313, p314)
        local _Magnitude = (Vector3.new(p314) - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
        local _TweenService2 = game:GetService('TweenService')

        tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(_Magnitude / p313, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
        tweenService = _TweenService2
        tweenx = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
            CFrame = CFrame.new(p314),
        })

        tweenx:Play()
        wait(_Magnitude / p313)
    end

    function TP(p319)
        Distance = (p319.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude

        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
        end

        pcall(function()
            local v320 = {CFrame = p319}

            tween = game:GetService('TweenService'):Create(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, TweenInfo.new(Distance / 210, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), v320)
        end)
        tween:Play()

        if Distance <= 250 then
            tween:Cancel()

            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = p319
        end
        if _G.StopTween == true then
            tween:Cancel()

            _G.Clip = false
        end
    end

        return math.floor((p321.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude)

    spawn(function()
        while wait() do
            if _G.Auto_Farm_Level then
                if _G.Select_Mode_Farm ~= 'Level Farm' then
                    if _G.Select_Mode_Farm ~= 'Fast Mode' then
                        if _G.Select_Mode_Farm == 'No Quest' then
                            pcall(function()
                                CheckLevel()

                                if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(Ms) then
                                    local v389, v390, v391 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:GetChildren())

                                    while true do
                                        local v392

                                        v391, v392 = v389(v390, v391)

                                        if v391 == nil then
                                            break
                                        end
                                        if v392:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (v392:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (v392.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (v392.Name == Ms and v392.Humanoid.Health > 0))) then
                                            repeat
                                                wait()
                                                EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                                                AutoHaki()

                                                PosMon = v392.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                                v392.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                                v392.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                                                v392.Head.CanCollide = false
                                                v392.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(50, 50, 50)
                                                StartMagnet = true

                                                TP(v392.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                                game:GetService('VirtualUser'):CaptureController()
                                                game:GetService('VirtualUser'):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))

                                        end
                                    end

                                    StartMagnet = false

                                    if game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(Ms) then
                                        TP(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(Ms).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0))
                                    else
                                        TP(CFrameMon)
                                    end
                                end
                            end)
                        end
                    else
                        pcall(function()
                            if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.SpawnPoint.Value ~= SPAWNPOINT then
                                repeat
                                    task.wait()
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head:Destroy()
                                    wait(0.5)

                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrameQuest

                                    game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('SetSpawnPoint')
                                until game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.SpawnPoint.Value == SPAWNPOINT

                                return
                            end
                            if not string.find(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, NameMon) then
                                StartMagnet = false

                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                            end
                            if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false then
                                StartMagnet = false

                                CheckLevel()
                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('StartQuest', NameQuest, LevelQuest)
                            end
                            if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= true then
                            end

                            CheckLevel()

                            if not game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(Ms) then
                                StartMagnet = false

                                if game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(Ms) then
                                    TP(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(Ms).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0))
                                else
                                    TP(CFrameMon)
                                end
                            end

                            local v393, v394, v395 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:GetChildren())

                            if true then
                                wait()

                                if string.find(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, NameMon) then
                                    EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                                    AutoHaki()

                                    PosMon = v396.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                    v396.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                    v396.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                                    v396.Head.CanCollide = false
                                    v396.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(50, 50, 50)
                                    StartMagnet = true

                                    TP(v396.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                    game:GetService('VirtualUser'):CaptureController()
                                    game:GetService('VirtualUser'):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
                                else
                                    StartMagnet = false

                                    game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                                end
                            end
                            if _G.Auto_Farm_Level and (v396.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v396.Parent) and game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= false then
                            end

                            local v396

                            v395, v396 = v393(v394, v395)

                            if v395 == nil then
                            end
                            if v396:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (v396:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (v396.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v396.Name == Ms)) then
                            else
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                else
                    pcall(function()
                        if not string.find(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, NameMon) then
                            StartMagnet = false

                            game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                        end
                        if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false then
                            StartMagnet = false

                            CheckLevel()

                            repeat
                                wait()
                                TP(CFrameQuest)
                            until (CFrameQuest.Position - game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 or not _G.Auto_Farm_Level

                            if (CFrameQuest.Position - game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 then
                                wait(1.2)
                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('StartQuest', NameQuest, LevelQuest)
                                wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end
                        if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= true then
                            return
                        end

                        CheckLevel()

                        if not game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(Ms) then

                            else
                                TP(CFrameMon)
                            end
                        end

                        if true then
                            wait()

                            if string.find(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, NameMon) then

                            end
                        end
                        if _G.Auto_Farm_Level and (v400.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v400.Parent) and game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= false then
                        end

                        end

                        else

                    end)

            end

    function EquipWeaponSword()
        pcall(function()
            local v402, v403, v404 = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v405

                v404, v405 = v402(v403, v404)

                if v404 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v405.ToolTip == 'Sword' and v405:IsA('Tool') then
                    local v406 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(v405.Name)

                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(v406)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    function EquipWeaponMelee()
        pcall(function()
            local v407, v408, v409 = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v410

                v409, v410 = v407(v408, v409)

                if v409 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v410.ToolTip == 'Melee' and v410:IsA('Tool') then
                    local v411 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(v410.Name)

                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(v411)
                end
            end
        end)
    end

                        }))

                    if Workspace.Map.Ice.Door.Transparency == 1 then
                        break
                    end
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Key') or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('Key') then
                        DoorNewWorldTween = TP(CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488).Position, CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488))

                        if (CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).magnitude <= 250 then
                            if DoorNewWorldTween then
                                DoorNewWorldTween:Stop()
                            end

                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488)

                            game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
                                'DressrosaQuestProgress',
                                'Detective',
                            }))
                            wait(0.5)

                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Key') then

                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(_Key)
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        AutoNewWorldTween = TP(CFrame.new(4849.29883, 5.65138149, 719.611877).Position, CFrame.new(4849.29883, 5.65138149, 719.611877))

                        if (CFrame.new(4849.29883, 5.65138149, 719.611877).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).magnitude <= 250 then
                            if DoorNewWorldTween then
                                DoorNewWorldTween:Stop()
                            end

                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4849.29883, 5.65138149, 719.611877)

                            game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
                                'DressrosaQuestProgress',
                                'Detective',

                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(_Key2)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                    break
                end
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Key') then
                    local _Key3 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Key')

                    wait(0.4)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(_Key3)
                end

                _G.DoorNewWorldTween = TP(CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488).Position, CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488))

                end

                _G.DoorNewWorldTween:Stop()

    spawn(function()
        pcall(function()
            while wait() do
                if _G.AutoFarmGunMastery then
                    local _Text3 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text

                    if not string.find(_Text3, NameMon) then
                        UseSkillGun = false
                        StartMasteryGunMagnet = false

                        game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                    end
                    if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= false then
                        if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true then
                            CheckLevel()

                            if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(Ms) then
                                pcall(function()
                                    local v521, v522, v523 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:GetChildren())

                                    while true do
                                        local v524

                                        v523, v524 = v521(v522, v523)

                                        if v523 == nil then
                                            return
                                        end
                                        if v524.Name == Ms then
                                            repeat
                                                if true then
                                                    task.wait()

                                                    if string.find(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, NameMon) then
                                                        HealthMin = v524.Humanoid.MaxHealth * _G.Kill_At / 100

                                                        if v524.Humanoid.Health > HealthMin then
                                                            UseSkillGun = false

                                                            AutoHaki()
                                                            EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)

                                                            v524.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
                                                            v524.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                                                            v524.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                                            v524.Head.CanCollide = false
                                                            v524.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(50, 50, 50)

                                                            TP(v524.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                                            game:GetService('VirtualUser'):CaptureController()
                                                            game:GetService('VirtualUser'):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
                                                        else
                                                            EquipWeapon(SelectToolWeaponGun)
                                                            TP(v524.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)

                                                            v524.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
                                                            v524.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                                                            v524.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                                            v524.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
                                                            v524.Head.CanCollide = false

                                                            local v525 = {
                                                                v524.HumanoidRootPart.Position,
                                                                v524.HumanoidRootPart,
                                                            }

                                                            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character[SelectToolWeaponGun].RemoteFunctionShoot:InvokeServer(unpack(v525))

                                                            UseSkillGun = true
                                                        end

                                                        StartMasteryGunMagnet = true

                                                        wait(0.2)

                                                        PosMonMasteryGun = v524.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame

                                                        game:GetService('VirtualUser'):CaptureController()
                                                        game:GetService('VirtualUser'):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
                                                    else
                                                        UseSkillGun = false
                                                        StartMasteryGunMagnet = false

                                                        TP(CFrameMon)
                                                        game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            until v524.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.AutoFarmGunMastery == false or game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false

                                            StartMasteryGunMagnet = false
                                            UseSkillGun = false
                                        end
                                    end
                                end)
                            else
                                StartMasteryGunMagnet = false
                                UseSkillGun = false

                                TP(CFrameMon)

                                local v526 = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(Ms)

                                if v526 then
                                    TP(v526.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(5, 35, 5))
                                elseif game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y <= 1 then
                                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = false
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        UseSkillGun = false
                        StartMasteryGunMagnet = false

                        CheckLevel()
                        TP(CFrameQuest)

                        if (CFrameQuest.Position - game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
                            task.wait()
                            game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('StartQuest', NameQuest, LevelQuest)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
    end)

    Main:Toggle('Auto Fram Boss Quest', false, function(p563)
        wait(0.1)
        game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
            'AbandonQuest',
        }))

        FarmBoss = p563

        while true do
            while true do
                if not FarmBoss then
                    return
                end

                wait(0.1)
                CheckLevelBoss()

                if SelectBoss == 'Don Swan [Lv. 1000] [Boss]' or (SelectBoss == 'Cursed Captain [Lv. 1325] [Raid Boss]' or (SelectBoss == 'Saber Expert [Lv. 200] [Boss]' or (SelectBoss == 'Mob Leader [Lv. 120] [Boss]' or SelectBoss == 'Darkbeard [Lv. 1000] [Raid Boss]'))) then
                    break
                end
                if SelectBoss ~= 'Order [Lv. 1250] [Raid Boss]' then
                    if SelectBoss ~= 'Rip_indra [Lv. 1500] [Boss]' then
                        if SelectBoss ~= 'Longma [Lv. 2000] [Boss]' then
                            if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) or game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) then
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= false then
                                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true then
                                        local v564, v565, v566 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                                        while true do
                                            local u567

                                            v566, u567 = v564(v565, v566)

                                            if v566 == nil then
                                                break
                                            end
                                            if FarmBoss and (u567.Humanoid.Health > 0 and u567.Name == MsBoss) then
                                                TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)

                                                repeat
                                                    wait()
                                                    pcall(function()
                                                        AutoHaki()

                                                        u567.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                                                        u567.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                                        u567.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)

                                                        TP(u567.HumanoidRootPart.Position, u567.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                                        EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                                                    end)
                                                until not FarmBoss or (u567.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false)
                                            end
                                        end

                                        TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
                                    end
                                else
                                    CheckLevelBoss()
                                    TP(CFrameQuestBoss, TweenSpeed)
                                    wait(1.5)
                                    game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('StartQuest', NaemQuestBoss, LevelQuestBoss)
                                    wait(1)
                                    TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) then
                            local v568, v569, v570 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                            while true do
                                local u571

                                v570, u571 = v568(v569, v570)

                                if v570 == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if FarmBoss and (u571:IsA('Model') and (u571:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (u571:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (u571.Humanoid.Health > 0 and u571.Name == MsBoss)))) then
                                    TP(u571.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)

                                    repeat
                                        wait()
                                        pcall(function()
                                            AutoHaki()

                                            u571.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                                            u571.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                            u571.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(80, 80, 80)

                                            TP(u571.HumanoidRootPart.Position, u571.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                            EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                                        end)
                                    until not FarmBoss or (not u571.Parent or u571.Humanoid.Health <= 0)
                                end
                            end
                        else
                            TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
                        end
                    elseif game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) then
                        local v572, v573, v574 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                        while true do
                            local u575

                            v574, u575 = v572(v573, v574)

                            if v574 == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if FarmBoss and (u575:IsA('Model') and (u575:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (u575:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (u575.Humanoid.Health > 0 and u575.Name == MsBoss)))) then
                                TP(u575.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)

                                repeat
                                    wait()
                                    pcall(function()
                                        AutoHaki()

                                        u575.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                                        u575.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                        u575.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(80, 80, 80)

                                        TP(u575.HumanoidRootPart.Position, u575.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)

                                    end)
                                until not FarmBoss or (not u575.Parent or u575.Humanoid.Health <= 0)
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
                    end
                elseif game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) then
                    local v576, v577, v578 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                    while true do
                        local u579

                        v578, u579 = v576(v577, v578)

                        if v578 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if FarmBoss and (u579:IsA('Model') and (u579:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (u579:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (u579.Humanoid.Health > 0 and u579.Name == MsBoss)))) then
                            TP(u579.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)

                            repeat
                                wait()
                                pcall(function()
                                    AutoHaki()

                                    u579.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                                    u579.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                    u579.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(80, 80, 80)

                                    TP(u579.HumanoidRootPart.Position, u579.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * MethodFarm)
                                    EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)

                                    Rig.CameraShakeInstance.CameraShakeState = {
                                        FadingIn = 3,
                                        FadingOut = 2,
                                        Sustained = 0,
                                        Inactive = 1,
                                    }
                                    RigC.activeController.timeToNextAttack = 0.5
                                end)
                            until not FarmBoss or (not u579.Parent or u579.Humanoid.Health <= 0)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
                end
            end

            if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild(SelectBoss) then
                break
            end

            TP(CFrameBoss, TweenSpeed)
        end

                u583.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                u583.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)

            end)
        end
        if FarmBoss and (u583.Parent and u583.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
        end

        local u583

        v582, u583 = v580(v581, v582)

        if v582 ~= nil then

    function Chest_100()
        local v607, v608, v609 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace'):GetChildren())

        while true do
            local v610

            v609, v610 = v607(v608, v609)

            if v609 == nil then
                break
            end
            if v610.Name == 'Chest1' and (v610.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 100 then
                _G.Chest_100 = v610

                return
            end
            if v610.Name == 'Chest2' and (v610.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 100 then
                _G.Chest_100 = v610

                        else
                            StartEctoplasmMagnet = false

                            if (Vector3.new(911.35827636719, 125.95812988281, 33159.5390625) - game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 18000 then

                    break
                end

                loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/BocusLuke/UI/main/STX/Module.Lua'))()

                local v695 = loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/BocusLuke/UI/main/STX/Client.Lua'))()

                wait(1)
                v695:Notify({

                    Description = 'You Have Max Observation',
                }, {
                    OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80),
                    Time = 5,
                    Type = 'option',
                }, {
                    Image = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=6023426923',
                    ImageColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 84, 84),

                        print(tostring(p696))
                    end,
                })
            end

            if not World2 then
            end
            if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Water Fighter [Lv. 1450]') then
                if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') then
                    repeat
                        task.wait()

                        game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Water Fighter [Lv. 1450]').HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(3, 0, 0)
                    until _G.AutoObservation == false or not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel')
                else
                    task.wait()

                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Water Fighter [Lv. 1450]').HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 0) + wait(1)

                    if not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') and _G.AutoObservation_Hop == true then
                        game:GetService('TeleportService'):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer)
                    end
                    if _G.AutoObservation ~= false and not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') then
                    end
                end
            else
                TP(CFrame.new(-3184.662353515625, 58.35300064086914, -9662.85546875))
            end
            if not World1 then
            end
            if game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Galley Captain [Lv. 650]') then
                if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') then
                    repeat
                        task.wait()

                        game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Galley Captain [Lv. 650]').HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(3, 0, 0)
                    until _G.AutoObservation == false or not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel')

                    wait(1)

                        game:GetService('TeleportService'):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer)
                    end
                    if _G.AutoObservation ~= false and not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') then
                    end
                end
            else
                TP(CFrame.new(5533.29785, 88.1079102, 4852.3916))
            end
            if not World3 then
            end
            if not game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Giant Islander [Lv. 1650]') then
            end
            if not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') then
            end

            repeat
                task.wait()

                game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Giant Islander [Lv. 1650]').HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(3, 0, 0)
            until _G.AutoObservation == false or not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel')

            TP(CFrame.new(4530.3540039063, 656.75695800781, -131.60952758789))
            task.wait()

            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace').Enemies:FindFirstChild('Giant Islander [Lv. 1650]').HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 0)

            wait(1)

            if not game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui:FindFirstChild('ImageLabel') and _G.AutoObservation_Hop == true then
                game:GetService('TeleportService'):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer)

    function MaterialMon()
        if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Radioactive Material' then
            if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Mystic Droplet' then
                if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Magma Ore' then
                    if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Angel Wings' then
                        if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Leather' then
                            if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Scrap Metal' then
                                if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Demonic Wisp' then
                                    if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Vampire Fang' then
                                        if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Conjured Cocoa' then
                                            if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Dragon Scale' then
                                                if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Gunpowder' then
                                                    if _G.SelectMaterial ~= 'Fish Tail' then
                                                        if _G.SelectMaterial == 'Mini Tusk' then
                                                            MMon = 'Mythological Pirate [Lv. 1850]'
                                                            MPos = CFrame.new(-13516.0458984375, 469.8182373046875, -6899.16064453125)
                                                            SP = 'BigMansion'
                                                        end
                                                    else
                                                        MMon = 'Fishman Captain [Lv. 1800]'
                                                        MPos = CFrame.new(-10961.0126953125, 331.7977600097656, -8914.29296875)
                                                        SP = 'PineappleTown'
                                                    end
                                                else
                                                    MMon = 'Pistol Billionaire [Lv. 1525]'
                                                    MPos = CFrame.new(-379.6134338378906, 73.84449768066406, 5928.5263671875)
                                                    SP = 'Default'
                                                end
                                            else
                                                MMon = 'Dragon Crew Warrior [Lv. 1575]'
                                                MPos = CFrame.new(5824.06982421875, 51.38640213012695, -1106.694580078125)
                                                SP = 'Hydra1'
                                            end
                                        else
                                            MMon = 'Chocolate Bar Battler [Lv. 2325]'
                                            MPos = CFrame.new(744.7930908203125, 24.76934242248535, -12637.7255859375)
                                            SP = 'Chocolate'
                                        end
                                    else
                                        MMon = 'Vampire [Lv. 975]'
                                        MPos = CFrame.new(-5999.20458984375, 6.437741279602051, -1290.059326171875)
                                        SP = 'Graveyard'
                                    end
                                else
                                    MMon = 'Demonic Soul [Lv. 2025]'
                                    MPos = CFrame.new(-9503.388671875, 172.139892578125, 6143.0634765625)
                                    SP = 'HauntedCastle'
                                end
                            elseif game.PlaceId ~= 2753915549 then
                                if game.PlaceId ~= 4442272183 then
                                    if game.PlaceId == 7449423635 then
                                        MMon = 'Pirate Millionaire [Lv. 1500]'
                                        MPos = CFrame.new(-289.6311950683594, 43.8282470703125, 5583.66357421875)
                                        SP = 'Default'
                                    end
                                else

                                    MPos = CFrame.new(-972.307373046875, 73.04473876953125, 1419.2901611328125)
                                    SP = 'DressTown'
                                end
                            else
                                MMon = 'Brute [Lv. 45]'
                                MPos = CFrame.new(-1132.4202880859375, 14.844913482666016, 4293.30517578125)
                                SP = 'Pirate'
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId ~= 2753915549 then
                            if game.PlaceId ~= 4442272183 then
                                if game.PlaceId == 7449423635 then
                                    MMon = 'Jungle Pirate [Lv. 1900]'
                                    MPos = CFrame.new(-11975.78515625, 331.7734069824219, -10620.0302734375)
                                    SP = 'PineappleTown'
                                end
                            else
                                MMon = 'Marine Captain [Lv. 900]'
                                MPos = CFrame.new(-2010.5059814453125, 73.00115966796875, -3326.620849609375)
                                SP = 'Greenb'
                            end
                        else
                            MMon = 'Pirate [Lv. 36]'
                            MPos = CFrame.new(-1211.8792724609375, 4.787090301513672, 3916.83056640625)
                            SP = 'Pirate'
                        end
                    else
                        MMon = 'Royal Soldier [Lv. 550]'
                        MPos = CFrame.new(-7827.15625, 5606.912109375, -1705.5833740234375)
                        SP = 'Sky2'
                    end
                elseif game.PlaceId ~= 2753915549 then
                    if game.PlaceId == 4442272183 then
                        MMon = 'Lava Pirate [Lv. 1200]'
                        MPos = CFrame.new(-5234.60595703125, 51.953372955322266, -4732.27880859375)

    spawn(function()
        pcall(function()
            while wait() do
                if _G.AutoQuestRace then
                    if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value ~= 'Human' then
                        if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value ~= 'Skypiea' then
                            if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value ~= 'Fishman' then
                                if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value ~= 'Cyborg' then
                                    if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value ~= 'Ghoul' then
                                        if game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value == 'Mink' then
                                            local v705, v706, v707 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace'):GetDescendants())

                                            while true do
                                                local v708

                                                v707, v708 = v705(v706, v707)

                                                if v707 == nil then
                                                    break
                                                end
                                                if v708.Name == 'StartPoint' then
                                                    getgenv().ToTargets(v708.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0))
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    else
                                        local v709, v710, v711 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetDescendants())

                                        while true do
                                            local u712

                                            v711, u712 = v709(v710, v711)

                                            if v711 == nil then
                                                break
                                            end
                                            if u712:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (u712:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and u712.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                                                pcall(function()
                                                    repeat
                                                        wait(0.1)

                                                        u712.Humanoid.Health = 0
                                                        u712.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false

                                                        sethiddenproperty(game.Players.LocalPlayer, 'SimulationRadius', math.huge)
                                                    until not _G.AutoQuestRace or (not u712.Parent or u712.Humanoid.Health <= 0)
                                                end)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                else
                                    getgenv().ToTargets(CFrame.new(28654, 14898.7832, -30, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1))
                                end
                            else

                pcall(function()
                    Mpoint = game.Players.localPlayer.Data.Stats.Melee.Level.Value
                    Dpoint = game.Players.localPlayer.Data.Stats.Defense.Level.Value
                    Dvilpoint = game.Players.localPlayer.Data.Stats['Demon Fruit'].Level.Value
                    stat = game.Players.localPlayer.Data.Points.Value

                                    1,
                                }))
                            end)
                        end

                            spawn(function()
                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
                                    'AddPoint',
                                    'Melee',
                                    1,
                                }))
                            end)

                        if Mpoint == 2200 and Dpoint <= 1800 then
                            spawn(function()
                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
                                    'AddPoint',
                                    'Defense',
                                    1,
                                }))
                            end)
                        end

                            spawn(function()
                                game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack({
                                    'AddPoint',
                                    'Demon Fruit',
                                    1,
                                }))
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
            if Mpoint == 2200 and (Dpoint >= 1800 and Dvilpoint >= 1500) then
                return
            end
        end
    end)

            pcall(function()

                    while true do
                        local v845

                        v844, v845 = v842(v843, v844)

                        if v844 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v845:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') then
                            if not v845:FindFirstChild('NpcEspes') then
                                local _BillboardGui10 = Instance.new('BillboardGui')
                                local _TextLabel20 = Instance.new('TextLabel')

                                _BillboardGui10.Parent = v845
                                _BillboardGui10.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling

                                _BillboardGui10.LightInfluence = 1

                                _BillboardGui10.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 2.5, 0)
                                _TextLabel20.Parent = _BillboardGui10
                                _TextLabel20.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                                _TextLabel20.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                _TextLabel20.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
                                _TextLabel20.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                                _TextLabel20.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 255)
                                _TextLabel20.Text.Size = 35
                            end

                            local v848 = math.floor((game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v845.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude)

                            v845.NpcEspes.TextLabel.Text = v845.Name .. ' - [' .. v848 .. ' M]'
                        end
                    end
                else
                    local v849, v850, v851 = pairs(game:GetService('Workspace').NPCs:GetChildren())

                    while true do
                        local v852

                        v851, v852 = v849(v850, v851)

                        if v851 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v852:FindFirstChild('NpcEspes') then
                            v852.NpcEspes:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end)

        _G.Raid = p862

    spawn(function()
        pcall(function()
            while wait() do
                if _G.Raid then
                    local v863, v864, v865 = pairs(game.Workspace.Enemies:GetDescendants())

                    while true do
                        local u866

                        v865, u866 = v863(v864, v865)

                        if v865 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if u866:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (u866:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and u866.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                            Pos = (u866.HumanoidRootPart.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude

                            if Pos <= 1000 then
                                pcall(function()
                                    repeat
                                        wait()

                                        u866.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                        u866.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(120, 120, 120)
                                        u866.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                                        u866.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                                        u866.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0

                                        EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                                        TPDOUN(u866.HumanoidRootPart.Position, u866.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 45, 0))
                                        game:GetService('VirtualUser'):CaptureController()
                                        game:GetService('VirtualUser'):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
                                    until not _G.Raid or (not u866.Parent or u866.Humanoid.Health <= 0) or not game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 1')
                                end)
                            end
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 5') then
                            Distance = (game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 5').Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            Speed = 150

                            local _TweenService11 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                            tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                            tweenService = _TweenService11
                            tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
                                CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 5').CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),
                            })

                            tween:Play()
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 4') then
                            Distance = (game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 4').Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            Speed = 150

                            local _TweenService12 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                            tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                            tweenService = _TweenService12
                            tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
                                CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 4').CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),
                            })

                            tween:Play()
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 3') then
                            Distance = (game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 3').Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            Speed = 150

                            local _TweenService13 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                            tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                            tweenService = _TweenService13
                            tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
                                CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 3').CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),
                            })

                            tween:Play()
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 2') then
                            Distance = (game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 2').Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            Speed = 150

                            local _TweenService14 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                            tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                            tweenService = _TweenService14
                            tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
                                CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 2').CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),
                            })

                            tween:Play()
                        elseif game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 1') then
                            Distance = (game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 1').Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            Speed = 150

                            local _TweenService15 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                            tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                            tweenService = _TweenService15
                            tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {
                                CFrame = game:GetService('Workspace')._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Island 1').CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),
                            })

                            tween:Play()
                        else

                                Lab2 = Vector3.new(-6438.73535, 250.645355, -4501.50684)

                                local _Magnitude10 = (Lab2 - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                local v873 = 150
                                local _TweenService16 = game:GetService('TweenService')

                                tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(_Magnitude10 / v873, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic)
                                tweenService = _TweenService16

                                    CFrame = CFrame.new(-6438.73535, 250.645355, -4501.50684),

                                _G.Clip = false

    local _LocalPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
    local _Value2 = _LocalPlayer.Character.Energy.Value

    function infinitestam()
        _LocalPlayer.Character.Energy.Changed:connect(function()
            if InfinitsEnergy then
                _LocalPlayer.Character.Energy.Value = _Value2
            end
        end)
    end

    spawn(function()
        while wait(0.1) do
            if InfinitsEnergy then
                wait(0.3)

                _Value2 = _LocalPlayer.Character.Energy.Value

                infinitestam()
            end
        end
    end)

    function getHits(p1029)
        local v1030 = workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()
        local v1031 = workspace.Characters:GetChildren()
        local v1032 = {}

        for v1033 = 1, #v1030 do
            local _Humanoid = v1030[v1033]:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')

            if _Humanoid then
                if _Humanoid.RootPart then
                    if _Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer:DistanceFromCharacter(_Humanoid.RootPart.Position) < p1029 + 5 then
                            table.insert(v1032, _Humanoid.RootPart)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        for v1035 = 1, #v1031 do
            local v1036 = v1031[v1035]

            if v1036 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character then
                local _Humanoid2 = v1036:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')

                if _Humanoid2 then
                    if _Humanoid2.RootPart then
                        if _Humanoid2.Health > 0 then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer:DistanceFromCharacter(_Humanoid2.RootPart.Position) < p1029 + 5 then
                                table.insert(v1032, _Humanoid2.RootPart)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        return v1032
    end

    function Attack()
        local _activeController = u1026.activeController

            task.spawn(function()
                if tick() - u1038 <= 0 then
                    game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').RigControllerEvent:FireServer('hit', getHits(5000), 10, '')
                else
                    _activeController:attack()

                    u1038 = tick()
                end
            end)
        end
    end

                            if _G.FastAttackNormalSpeed then
                                function u1058.play() end

                                p1060:Play(2.1, 2.1, 2.1)
                                p1064(v1065)

                                u1058.play = shared.cpc

                                wait(p1060.length * 0.5)
                                p1060:Stop()
                            else
                                p1064(v1065)

                                u1058.play = shared.cpc

                                wait(p1060.length * 0.5)
                                p1060:Stop()
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end)
    end)

    local u1066 = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.Util.CameraShaker)

    CombatFrameworkR = require(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts.CombatFramework)
    y = debug.getupvalues(CombatFrameworkR)[2]

    spawn(function()
        game:GetService('RunService').RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            if _G.FastAttack and typeof(y) == 'table' then
                pcall(function()
                    u1066:Stop()

                    y.activeController.timeToNextAttack = math.huge ^ math.huge ^ math.huge
                    y.activeController.timeToNextAttack = 0
                    y.activeController.hitboxMagnitude = 2048
                    y.activeController.active = false
                    y.activeController.timeToNextBlock = 0
                    y.activeController.focusStart = 1655503339.0980349
                    y.activeController.increment = 1
                    y.activeController.blocking = false
                    y.activeController.attacking = false
                    y.activeController.humanoid.AutoRotate = true
                end)
            end
        end)
    end)

    return
end
